---
name: Open Bank Project
x-slug: open-bank-project
description: The Open Bank Project is an open source API and App store for banks that
  empowers financial institutions to securely and rapidly enhance their digital offerings
  using an ecosystem of 3rd party applications and services.

- name: Open Bank Project
  x-api-slug: open-bank-project
  description: The Open Bank Project is an open source API and App store for banks
    that empowers financial institutions to securely and rapidly enhance their digital
    offerings using an ecosystem of 3rd party applications and services.
